***сталкер.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сталкер.html>ста́лкер</a> (4769)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>The word was coined by the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Strugatsky_brothers" class="extiw" title="w:Strugatsky brothers">Strugatsky brothers</a> for their novel "<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Roadside_Picnic" class="extiw" title="w:Roadside Picnic">Roadside Picnic</a>" (1972), as an allusion to <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Rudyard_Kipling" class="extiw" title="w:Rudyard Kipling">Rudyard Kipling</a>'s character <i>Stalky</i> from the "<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Stalky_%26_Co." class="extiw" title="w:Stalky amp; Co.">Stalky amp; Co.</a>" stories and the <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">stalker</i>. <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ста́лки</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">Stálki</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> was well remembered by the Strugatskys from their childhood, when they read the stories in Russian translation. In the "Roadside Picnic", <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сталкер.html>ста́лкер</a></b> was a common nickname for men engaged in the illegal trade of prospecting for and smuggling of alien artifacts from the mysterious and dangerous "Zone".
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сталкер.html>ста́лкер</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stálker</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сталкер.html>ста́лкера</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сталкер.html>ста́лкеры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сталкер.html>ста́лкеров</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ста́лкерша</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">rare</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> stalker <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a person who stalks game</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span> (<i>see usage notes</i>)</li>
<li>any person, whose occupation or activity is dangerously similar to those of characters from "Roadside Picnic".
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чернобыльский.html>черно́быльский</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сталкер.html>ста́лкер</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">černóbylʹskij <b>stálker</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">a Chernobyl stalker, a guide to the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Zone_of_alienation" class="extiw" title="w:Zone of alienation">Zone of alienation</a> near Chernobyl</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ста́лкерский</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">stálkerskij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ста́лкерство</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">stálkerstvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>It's a traditional translation, although not very accurate in meaning and connotations and it's seldom used in the sense of "stalker".</li>
<li>The term was popularised by 1979 <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Andrey_Tarkovsky" class="extiw" title="w:Andrey Tarkovsky">Andrey Tarkovsky</a>'s ((андре́й Тарковсќий) movie with the same name - <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Stalker_(1979_film)" class="extiw" title="w:Stalker (1979 film)">Stalker</a></i> (Russian: <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сталкер.html>ста́лкер</a></span>).</li>
<li>The English term "stalker" (a person who secretly follows someone, sometimes with unlawful intentions) is usually described as <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:упорный.html>упо́рный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:преследователь.html>пресле́дователь</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">upórnyj preslédovatelʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">persistent follower</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́к</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:который.html>кото́рый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>идёт</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пята.html>пята́м</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">čelovék, kotóryj idjót po pjatám</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">person who comes on the heels</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to bring together

<li>to cause to collide</li></ol>

***сталкиваться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сталкиваться.html>ста́лкиваться</a> (5338)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сталкивать.html>ста́лкивать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stálkivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сталкиваться.html>ста́лкиваться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stálkivatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:столкнуться.html>столкну́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to collide (with), to run (into), to bump (into), to come across (with) (<a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> - with)</li>
<li>to face, to be confronted with
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сталкиваться.html>ста́лкиваться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:трудность.html>тру́дностями</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>stálkivatʹsja</b> s trúdnostjami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to face / to be confronted with difficulties</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сталкивать.html>ста́лкивать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stálkivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

***сталь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сталь.html>сталь</a> (8213)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Stahl</i> and/or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">staal</i>, both “steel”.
</p>

***стамеска.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стамеска.html>стаме́ска</a> (29099)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Stemmeisen</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стамеска.html>стаме́ска</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">staméska</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стамеска.html>стаме́ски</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стамеска.html>стаме́ски</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стамеска.html>стаме́сок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>(wood) chisel <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">tool consisting of a slim oblong block of metal</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">долбёжная <b><a href = vnd.unilang:стамеска.html>стаме́ска</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">dolbjóžnaja <b>staméska</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">carving chisel</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***стан.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стан.html>стан</a> (9960)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">станъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stanŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*stanъ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*steh₂-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стан.html>стан</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stan</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стан.html>ста́на</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стан.html>ста́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стан.html>ста́нов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>figure, stature, torso
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тонкий.html>то́нкий</a> <strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:стан.html>ста́н</a></strong></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">tónkij stán</i> ― <span class="e-translation">slender waist</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>camp, campground
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полевой.html>полево́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стан.html>ста́н</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">polevój stán</i> ― <span class="e-translation">camp</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передвижной.html>передвижно́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:полевой.html>полево́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стан.html>ста́н</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">peredvižnój polevój stán</i> ― <span class="e-translation">mobile field station</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>side, camp
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стан.html>ста́н</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мятежник.html>мяте́жников</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">stán mjatéžnikov</i> ― <span class="e-translation">rebeldom</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вражеский.html>вра́жеский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стан.html>ста́н</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vrážeskij stán</i> ― <span class="e-translation">hostile camp</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стан.html>ста́не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:враг.html>врага́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v stáne vragá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">in the enemy's camp</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нотный.html>но́тный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стан.html>ста́н</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nótnyj stán</i> ― <span class="e-translation">staff, stave</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>mill, machine
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">загото́вочный <a href = vnd.unilang:стан.html>ста́н</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zagotóvočnyj stán</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:бар.html>bar</a> mill</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">обжи́мный <a href = vnd.unilang:стан.html>ста́н</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">obžímnyj stán</i> ― <span class="e-translation">blooming</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">листопрока́тный <a href = vnd.unilang:стан.html>ста́н</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">listoprokátnyj stán</i> ― <span class="e-translation">flatting-mill</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">прока́тный <a href = vnd.unilang:стан.html>ста́н</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">prokátnyj stán</i> ― <span class="e-translation">rolling mill, train</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">сталепрока́тный <a href = vnd.unilang:стан.html>ста́н</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">staleprokátnyj stán</i> ― <span class="e-translation">steel-rolling mill</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">трубопрока́тный <a href = vnd.unilang:стан.html>ста́н</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">truboprokátnyj stán</i> ― <span class="e-translation">tube mill</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проволочный.html>про́волочный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стан.html>ста́н</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">próvoločnyj stán</i> ― <span class="e-translation">wire mill</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">рельсопрока́тный <a href = vnd.unilang:стан.html>ста́н</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">relʹsoprokátnyj stán</i> ― <span class="e-translation">rail-mill</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стандарт.html>станда́рт</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">standárt</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стандарт.html>станда́рта</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стандарт.html>станда́рты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стандарт.html>станда́ртов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>standard (level of quality)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:станица.html>стани́ца</a> (10513)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology is missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:станица.html>стани́ца</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">staníca</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:станица.html>стани́цы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:станица.html>стани́цы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:станица.html>стани́ц</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Cossack village, stanitsa</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Villages are often called <b><a href = vnd.unilang:станица.html>стани́ца</a></b> in typically Cossack regions, such as Don, Kuban (Rostov oblast, Krasnodar kray, Stavropol kray, etc.)</li></ul>

***становиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:становиться.html>станови́ться</a> (430)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Nasal present of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стать.html>стать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">statʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. See also <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*stati</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:становиться.html>станови́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stanovítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стать.html>стать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to stand, to take a stand</li>
<li>to get, to become, to grow</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:становление.html>становле́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stanovlénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:становление.html>становле́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:становление.html>становле́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:становление.html>становле́ний</a></b>)

***станок.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:станок.html>стано́к</a> (5037)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стан.html>стан</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stan</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о́к</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ók</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:станок.html>стано́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stanók</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:станок.html>станка́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:станок.html>станки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:станок.html>станко́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>machine, lathe, press
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:печатный.html>печа́тный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:станок.html>стано́к</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pečátnyj <b>stanók</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">printing press</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>mount, mounting, bench</li>
<li>support, prop, easel</li>
<li>safety razor</li></ol>

<p><a href = vnd.unilang:общий.html>О́бщее</a> прототипическое <a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>значе́ние</a> — <i><a href = vnd.unilang:приспособление.html>приспособле́ние</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:обеспечивающий.html>обеспе́чивающее</a> чему-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:стабильность.html>стаби́льность</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:опора.html>опо́ру</a></i>.

<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">Фрезерный <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:станок.html>стано́к</a></span>. </span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:станционный.html>станцио́нный</a> (16189)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:станция.html>ста́нция</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stáncija</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о́нный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ónnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:станционный.html>станцио́нный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stanciónnyj</span>) (<i>no comparative</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> station <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">railway, broadcasting, space, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:станционный.html>станцио́нный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:смотритель.html>смотри́тель</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>stanciónnyj</b> smotrítelʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">stationmaster</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:станционный.html>станцио́нная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:плотина.html>плоти́на</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>stanciónnaja</b> plotína</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>station</b> dam <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a dam combined with a water pumping station</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational<span class="ib-comma">,</span> telephony</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> office, exchange
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:станционный.html>станцио́нное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:повреждение.html>поврежде́ние</a></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">telephony</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>stanciónnoje</b> povreždénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>office</b> fault, <b>exchange</b> fault</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational<span class="ib-comma">,</span> rail transport</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> yard</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> power plant</li></ol>

***станция.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:станция.html>ста́нция</a> (884)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>A conflation of two sources — Russian archaic <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стан.html>стан</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stan</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">postal station, stage</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:станица.html>стани́ца</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">staníca</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stanitsa</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and the European words for “station” descended from Latin <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">statio</i>, such as Polish <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">stacja</i>, French <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">station</i>, Italian <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">stazione</i>, etc. Both sources ultimately derive from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*steh₂-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:станция.html>ста́нция</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stáncija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:станция.html>ста́нции</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:станция.html>ста́нции</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:станция.html>ста́нций</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>station
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">широковеща́тельная <b><a href = vnd.unilang:станция.html>ста́нция</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">širokoveščátelʹnaja <b>stáncija</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">broadcast station</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:космический.html>косми́ческая</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:станция.html>ста́нция</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kosmíčeskaja <b>stáncija</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">space station</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:железнодорожный.html>железнодоро́жная</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:станция.html>ста́нция</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">železnodoróžnaja <b>stáncija</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">railway station</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">электро<b><a href = vnd.unilang:станция.html>ста́нция</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">elektro<b>stáncija</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">power station</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:радио.html>ра́дио</a><b><a href = vnd.unilang:станция.html>ста́нция</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">radio<b>stáncija</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">radio station</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">автозапра́вочная <b><a href = vnd.unilang:станция.html>ста́нция</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">avtozaprávočnaja <b>stáncija</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">gas station, filling station</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">telephony</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> office, exchange</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">rail transport</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> yard</li>
<li>power plant</li></ol>

***старательный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:старательный.html>стара́тельный</a> (3325)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">стара́ть(ся)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">starátʹ(sja)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тельный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-telʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:старательный.html>стара́тельный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">starátelʹnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)стара́тельнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)стара́тельней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>assiduous, diligent, hard-working

***стараться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стараться.html>стара́ться</a> (488)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*starati sę</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">стара́тися</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">starátysja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bulgarian language">Bulgarian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg"><a href = vnd.unilang:старый.html>стара́я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сей.html>сё</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">starája se</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh">ста̏рати <a href = vnd.unilang:сей.html>сё</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to try to achieve; to try</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (1sg. <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh">ста̏ра̄м <a href = vnd.unilang:сей.html>сё</a></i>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovene_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovene language">Slovene</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">stȃrati se</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">tonal orthography</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">starat se</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovak_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovak language">Slovak</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sk">starať sa</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">starać się</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Upper_Sorbian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Upper Sorbian language">Upper Sorbian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="hsb">starać so</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lower_Sorbian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lower Sorbian language">Lower Sorbian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dsb">staraś se</i>. Related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Russian language">Russian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:страда.html>страда́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stradá</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">harvest</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (originally "hard work"), <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:страдать.html>страда́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stradátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to suffer</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. More distantly cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">starìnti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to pull with difficulty</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (1sg. <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">starinù</i>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latvian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Latvian language">Latvian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lv">starîgs</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">zealous</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Prussian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Old Prussian language">Old Prussian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="prg">stūrnawiskan</i> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">seriousness, importance</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span>, <span class="ann-pos">ins. sg.</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">stierne</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">serious, strict</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">sternāx</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">absurd</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">strēnuus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">active</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (also per Vasmer <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cōnsternō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to shake</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, inf. <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cōnsternāre</i>, not <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cōnsternere</i>, which is a different verb), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">στρηνής</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">strēnḗs</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hard, sharp</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">στρῆνος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">strênos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">force</span><span title="w:Welsh language">Welsh</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cy">trîn</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span <hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стараться.html>стара́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">starátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:постараться.html>постара́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to try, to attempt
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:стараться.html>стара́юсь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:думать.html>ду́мать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:другой.html>други́х</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хороший.html>хоро́ших</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:фильм.html>фи́льмах</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja <b>starájusʹ</b> dúmatʹ o drugíx xoróšix fílʹmax.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I'm trying to think of other good movies.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to endeavour/endeavor, to make an effort</li>
<li>to pursue</li>
<li>to strive</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><a href = vnd.unilang:стараться.html>Стара́ться</a> refers to a continued effort of trying, as opposed to a single attempt. For the act of trying a single time, see <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробовать.html>про́бовать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">próbovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробовать.html>про́бовать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">próbovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стареть.html>старе́ть</a> (7849)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стареть.html>старе́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">starétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:постареть.html>постаре́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:устареть.html>устаре́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to grow old, to age, to advance in age
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:постареть.html>постаре́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">postarétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to become out of date
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:устареть.html>устаре́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ustarétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:старец.html>ста́рец</a> (8175)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*starьcь</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:старый.html>ста́рый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stáryj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ец</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ec</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:старец.html>ста́рец</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stárec</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:старец.html>ста́рца</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:старец.html>ста́рцы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:старец.html>ста́рцев</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стариться.html>ста́рившийся</a> (29365)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стариться.html>ста́рившийся</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stárivšijsja</span>)
</p>

***старик.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:старик.html>старик</a> (316)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">старий</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">starij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">stařík</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:старик.html>стари́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">starík</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:старик.html>старика́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:старик.html>старики́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:старик.html>старико́в</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:старуха.html>стару́ха</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>old man</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> old-timer, that man who has worked or served somewhere more than his younger colleagues</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> father, foozle</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> elderly husband for a wife</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> address</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> chap</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:старикан.html>старика́н</a> (21473)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:старик.html>стари́к</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">starík</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́н</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-án</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
